 This scientist has developed an Artificial Intelligence Technique named RF Capture so that a human standing on the other side of the wall can also be seen through the wifi router signal
 is takanic se aisi chijen bhi dikh sakati hai jo hame nagn aankh se dikhaai nahin deteen
 This is how RF capturerf Capture uses wifi signal to work
 jaise vaaifai signal diwaar ke duusari taraf aasaani se ja saktaa he, vaise hi yah bhi uske saath diwaar kii duusari taraf jaataa he
 As soon as the signal hits the person standing on the other side, it reflects and returns to this device again
 is prakriya ke baad riflact kiye gaye body parts ko jod kar yah pataa lagaaya ja saktaa he ki diwaar ke us paar koun khadaa he or wo kya kar rahaa he
 Think of it like RF Capture can go to the other side of any physical object through the radio wave
 The radio signal collides with any person or object standing on the other side and returns to the RF capture
 Can be imaged

 ) China on Wednesday launched its most powerful naval warship - the Type 055 - one of the world's largest warships
 china is tarah ke chaar yudhpot taiyaar kar rahaa he, jinamein se pehla buudhvaar subah shanghai pot par saarvajanik rup se pradarshit kiya gaya

 bharat ke atyaadhunik yupoton kaa vazan bhi puri tarah sashastr kar die jane par 8,200 ton rahane vaala he, or unhen sataha se hawa main maar kar sakane vaali, anti-ship tathaa land atake karne main sakasham kul milakar 50 mixilon se las kiya ja sakegaa

 " Total Dhamaal, the third film of the Dhamaal series, will now be released by next year
 isaki relies date lagaataar aage bad rahi he
 Recently, Ajay Devgn has tweeted that the release date of his upcoming film Total Dhamaal has now changed
 film ' de de pyaar de' kii bhi relies date bhi badali gai he
 Now both these films will be released next year
 ajay ne bataaya ki film main VFX ke kaam kii vajah se film kii relies main deree ho rahi he
 Let me tell you that the film Total Dhamaal was earlier released on 7 December 2018, now it will be released on 22 February 2019 next year
 is film kaa nirdesan indra kumaar kar rahe hai
 In this film, apart from Ajay Devgan, Anil Kapoor, Madhuri Dixit, Ritesh Deshmukh will be seen in the lead roles
 December date with you’ll looks challenging, but still keeping my Feb date!due to extensive VFX work, Total Dhamaal will now release on 22nd Feb and De De Pyaar De moves to 26th April
 - Ajay Devgn (@ajaydevgn) October 25, 2018 According to DNA report, Ajay Devgan and Prakash Jhane have joined hands for this new project and now the casting and location of the film is in the works
 jaise hi sab tay ho jayega is film kii ghoshnaa kar di jayega
